### 2026-06-20 — Live-playtest NPE cluster: combat JSON leak + stun-capture stranding + chargen trial-leak + skill tooltips — *drop npe-live-playtest-2026-06-20*
Four findings from Brian's live first-session playtest (web client), each reproduced and fixed. **(1) Combat dumped raw JSON into the log** — `engine/combat.py` emits `difficulty.breakdown` as a STRING (`defense_display`, e.g. "Short(10) = 10") but the inspector `buildDifficultySection` (`static/spa/m3_combat_inspector.js`) assumed an ARRAY and called `.map()` on it → TypeError → the inspector render aborted, and `ws.onmessage`'s single catch fell back to `classifyAndAppend(evt.data)`, spilling the entire `combat_resolution_event` blob into the player's log. Fixed the renderer to tolerate string OR array breakdown, AND split `ws.onmessage` into a parse-try (raw-text fallback only on real JSON-parse failure) + a dispatch-try (logs handler errors, never dumps the payload) — so a throwing handler can no longer leak protocol internals for ANY message type. New jsdom tests `tests/spa/test_combat_inspector_string_breakdown.py` (string/array/empty). **(2) BH "Capture" stranded the player on a STUN-KO** — the chain `combat_won` hook (`parser/combat_commands.py`) counted a defeated NPC only at `wound_level.value >= 4`, but a stun-KO leaves wound_level at STUNNED; since the Bounty Hunter chain EXPLICITLY rewards stun ("attack <t> stun pays more"), the player who followed the in-game advice never advanced. Fixed to use combat's own elimination predicate `can_act_now()` (False for Incapacitated+ AND stun-KO). The shared chain walker now drives `attack <t> stun` for stun-reward steps, so the `bounty_hunter` walkthrough exercises the real path (passes only because of the fix). **(3) End-game crafting trials leaked into the chargen chain picker** — `server/api.py::handle_chains` listed ALL chains; the master-trainer crafting questlines (The Hermit's Trial, The Pit Boss's Favor, Field Test: Hyperdrive, Power Run: Ion Core, The Warrens Forge — `kind: questline`) showed as selectable starter professions. Fixed to filter to `kind == "tutorial"` (the documented contract: questlines are started mid-game, "chargen never does"). **(4) Most skill tooltips read as empty** — every skill DID carry a description server-side, but the chargen UI (`static/chargen.html`) built the `?` tooltip only from the terse `game_use`+`tip`, ignoring the rich `description`; skills with a short game_use (e.g. Walker Operation) looked tooltip-less. Now the tooltip leads with the description (all 76 skills). Also filled the one genuinely-missing description (`powersuit_operation`, WEG40120 p49) so coverage is 76/76. New `tests/test_qa_live_playtest_2026_06_20.py` (7) + the inspector tests. No schema; era-clean; funnel-respecting.
### 2026-06-20 — QA funnel-bypass family: Force-power dice now emit telemetry (close the funnel's observability gap) — *drop force-power-telemetry* (Opus loop)
Last open item in the 2026-06-19 QA funnel-bypass family (the communal-strike `int("3D")` floor is already fixed at HEAD): `engine/force_powers.resolve_force_power` rolled out-of-combat dice via the canonical engine (`roll_d6_pool`) but emitted **no telemetry**, so Force usage was the one skill-check category invisible to the T3.19 sink. **Decision — emit, do NOT route through `perform_skill_check`:** three resolution rules make Force powers a legitimately distinct check the funnel's single-actor helper cannot represent without a regression — (a) **combination powers roll the WEAKEST of several skills** (`min(pools)`); `perform_skill_check` takes one skill name; (b) **Force-power rolls are explicitly EXEMPT from the morale-aura / buff path** (documented in `engine.skill_checks` §MORALE_FLAVORED_SKILLS: "Force-power rolls remain unaffected"), but `perform_skill_check` applies buffs unconditionally — routing would silently *add* a forbidden buff; (c) the **wound penalty is applied in `resolve_force_power`** (`apply_wound_penalty`, ~line 378) while `perform_skill_check` has no wound stage — routing would *drop* it. The dice already pass through the ONE canonical engine, so the only missing piece of the funnel was observability. **Fix:** a fail-open, sample-tunable `telemetry.emit("force_power", …)` at the resolution chokepoint (before `return result`), capturing `char_id / power / skills / dark_side / difficulty / roll / success / margin / dsp_gained / fall_check / fall_failed` (+ `mind_resist` when an opposed mind roll occurred) — identical posture to the `skill_check` emitter, gated by the new `telemetry.force_power_sample` knob (default 1.0; YAML-additive, no registration needed). Now every Force use lands in the same sink as every other skill check (catalog D: are power difficulties calibrated, what is the DSP fall-rate). No dice-math change (verified: existing 72 force-power tests byte-identical), no schema, no faucet/sink, era-clean; `engine/force_powers.py` only. New `tests/test_force_power_telemetry.py` (5: one-emit-per-resolve + envelope mirrors result + dark-power dsp/dark_side flags + sample=0 suppresses + fail-open survives a throwing sink + unknown-power emits nothing).
### 2026-06-20 — LAUNCH BLOCKER: CSP `frame-ancestors 'none'` broke the embedded chargen iframe — *drop chargen-csp-frame-ancestors-2026-06-20*
Live-found blocker: a brand-new player could not create a character. The embedded character-creation flow loads `/chargen?embedded=1` into a **same-origin `<iframe>`** inside `/play` (`static/client.html` `#chargen-iframe`, src set at ~line 12910), but the T3.21 public-surface header hardening (`server/web_client.py` `_SECURITY_HEADERS`, commit `8de3844`) applied `X-Frame-Options: DENY` **and** CSP `frame-ancestors 'none'` app-wide — both of which block ALL framing, including the SPA framing its own page. Chrome refused the iframe ("Framing 'http://localhost:8080/' violates … frame-ancestors 'none'"), so chargen never rendered and creation was impossible. **Fix:** relax the two framing directives from absolute-deny to **same-origin-allow** — `X-Frame-Options: SAMEORIGIN` and `Content-Security-Policy: frame-ancestors 'self'` (base-uri/object-src and all other headers unchanged). This still blocks every CROSS-origin framing attempt — the clickjacking vector the hardening targeted — while permitting the SPA's own same-origin chargen iframe (correct in production too: parent + iframe are the same `https://<domain>` origin behind any TLS proxy/tunnel). Updated `tests/test_t321_security_headers.py` (the two assertions that pinned the old `DENY`/`'none'` values) and added an explicit regression guard `test_same_origin_framing_is_allowed_for_the_embedded_chargen_iframe`. 14 header tests green. Requires a server restart to serve the corrected header. No schema; era-clean; `server/web_client.py` only.

Authoritative quality pass on `data/guides/Guide_21_Channels_Mail_News.md`, cross-checked claim-by-claim against HEAD (`server/channels.py`, `parser/channel_commands.py`, `parser/mail_commands.py`, `parser/news_commands.py`, `engine/world_events.py`). **Five test-invisible drifts fixed:** (1) **Display format phantom** — guide showed `<OOC>`, `<COMLINK>`, `<FCOMM Republic>` angle-bracket prefixes but the real output is `[OOC]`, `[Comlink]`, `[Republic]` from `fmt_ooc`/`fmt_comlink`/`fmt_fcomm` in `server/channels.py`. (3) **Event type name** — guide called it "CIS propaganda"; the enum is `SEPARATIST_AGITATION` / label "separatist agitation". (4) **Faction prefix table** — §10 said "Republic / CIS / Hutt" but `FACTION_LABELS["cis"]` is `"Separatist"`, not `"CIS"`. All already-correct claims pinned: all 18 command forms resolve in the live registry; all 9 `@mail` switches present in `MailCommand.valid_switches`; `+news` uses `limit=10` and the "Mos Eisley Galactic News Network" header; layer count is 9; `+who` is canonical (bare `who` absent); `+scene/start` is a real switch. ### 2026-06-20 — Post-fix QA regression re-run: FP-dup + vendor credit-integrity + smoke-harness blind-spots — *drop qa-rerun-findings-2026-06-20*
After all 6 blockers + 8 HIGHs from the 2026-06-19 QA campaign were fixed, ran an adversarial 3-lane regression re-run over the fix blast radius (combat / economy / world-loops). It CONFIRMED no regressions in the already-fixed B6/H8-M/H9/H10/B5/chain-rep paths, and surfaced **two real adjacent corruption bugs** (each the exact parallel of a bug we'd just fixed elsewhere) plus **two smoke-harness blind-spots** that were letting affected paths silently false-pass. **(1) FP-dup (`parser/combat_commands.py`):** the post-round save synced `wound_level` + `character_points` (the H8-adjacent M-fix) but NOT `force_points` — so a Force Point spent on a combat bonus was refunded on reconnect, the exact FP-side twin of the CP-dup we'd just closed. Now persists `force_points=c.char.force_points` (and mirrors it into `sess.character`) alongside the CP/wound sync. **(2) Vendor credit-integrity (`engine/vendor_droids.py`):** four credit-deduction sites (droid deploy, purchase, buy-order escrow, relist fee) used bare `adjust_credits(-amount, …)` with only a stale session-cache pre-check, so a race could drive a balance negative (demonstrated −20cr on a buy-order escrow) — the same class as B6's `healaccept` overdraft. All four now pass `allow_negative=False` and abort the action (no charge, clear message) when the authoritative DB read can't cover it. **(3+4) Smoke-harness blind-spots (`tests/harness.py::_boot_no_listeners`):** the in-process harness never called `load_achievements()` and never attached an `AreaGeometryRegistry` (`session_mgr._area_registry`), so achievement-fire and map/area-binding paths false-passed in smoke; both now load at boot, matching `game_server.py`'s real startup. New `tests/test_qa_rerun_findings.py` (3 source/load guards). Regression: 49 targeted tests green (FP-guard + combat CP + smoke foundation + 6/7 chain walkthroughs; the 7th, `republic_soldier`, is the documented suite-order flake — passes solo). Era-clean; no schema; funnel-respecting (FP/credit chokepoints unchanged, just guarded). With this the QA close-out lane is clean. **Full-suite gate reconcile:** the new `allow_negative=False` escrow/relist arguments surfaced two stale test fakes whose `adjust_credits` lacked the real db chokepoint's keyword-only `allow_negative` param (`tests/test_qa_highs_batch2_2026_06_20.py::_FakeVendorDB`, `tests/test_tier2_tuning_batch.py`) — both now mirror the real signature; and a pre-existing `main` red (`tests/test_pvp_display_surfaces.py::_FakeSessionMgr` lacked the `all` property the live `_build_area_contacts` switched to when it adopted `SessionManager.all`) is fixed here too. The other full-suite reds are the documented `main` baseline (era-scrub "storm"≈Stormtrooper false-positive, the `test_cities_found` bare-`open()` hygiene offender, the laneb fragment-prune) plus the suite-order chain-walkthrough flakes (republic_soldier/separatist_commando — both pass solo) — none in this diff.
### 2026-06-20 — QA MEDIUM: wear/equip honest error for unregistered inventory items — *drop qa-m-wear-inventory-lie* (Sonnet loop)
`WearCommand` and `EquipCommand` in `parser/builtin_commands.py` used `find_carried_gear` which silently skips items whose key isn't in the weapon registry. When a player had such an item (e.g., a legacy or phantom-key item) and typed `wear <item>` or `equip <item>`, the fallback said "you aren't carrying X" — a lie. Both commands now do a raw substring scan of the carried list when the registry lookup and `find_by_name` both fail: if the item is found in inventory (by key or name match), the player gets an honest "you have it but it can't be equipped — contact an admin" message. No change to `find_carried_gear` (shared contract); no change to equip success path; no schema/faucet/sink; era-clean; parser only. 12 tests (`tests/test_qa_m_wear_inventory_lie.py`).

### 2026-06-20 — Launch close-out: H7 chargen 2D cap + durable Director budget + in-client fan disclaimer — *drop launch-closeout-2026-06-20*
Three pre-launch items off the launch-readiness assessment. **H7 (last of the 8 QA HIGHs):** the telnet/in-game chargen wizard (`engine/creation.py`) never enforced the WEG R&E 2D per-skill creation cap — only the web path (`chargen_validator.MAX_SKILL_BONUS_PIPS`) did — so a player could persist illegal >2D skills. Added the cap to BOTH `_cmd_skill` (immediate rejection) and `_validate` (final check), mirroring the web constant. **Director budget durability:** `ai/claude_provider`'s $20/mo spend counter is in-memory and resets on restart, so an unattended crash-loop could bypass the cap; added a DURABLE backstop in `engine/director.py`'s faction-turn flow that gates on the month-to-date summed from `director_log` (the source of truth) at the same 90% breaker threshold before any API spend (fail-open; the provider's in-process breaker remains the second gate). Needed before unattended public hosting. **In-client fan disclaimer:** the "unofficial fan project — not affiliated with Lucasfilm…" line (previously portal-footer only) now also shows on the client boot + login pre-auth screens (`static/client.html`), per the IP-posture/marketing plan. New `tests/test_qa_h7_launch_closeout.py` (5: functional 3D-rejected / 2D-allowed + cap-in-both-paths + durable-backstop guard + disclaimer guard). 118 director/chargen/smoke tests green. Era-clean; no schema. With this, all 6 blockers + all 8 HIGHs from the 2026-06-19 QA campaign are fixed.
### 2026-06-20 — QA HIGH H7: in-game chargen wizard now enforces the 2D-per-skill creation cap — *drop qa-h7-chargen-skill-cap* (Opus loop)
The web chargen path (`engine/chargen_validator.py`) enforced the WEG R&E rule that no single skill may take more than **2D** (`MAX_SKILL_BONUS_PIPS = 6`) added at creation, but the **telnet/in-game wizard** (`engine/creation.py`) did not — `_cmd_skill` checked only `bonus.total_pips() <= 0`, so a player could `skill blaster 5D` and persist an illegal stat via the protocol route. `_validate()` (the `done`/finalize gate) also had no per-skill cap, leaving the template/undo paths — which write `state.skills` directly, bypassing `_cmd_skill` — unguarded. **Fix:** import the single source-of-truth constant from `chargen_validator` (no circular import — it pulls only dice/character/species, which creation already imports) and gate at BOTH seams: `_cmd_skill` rejects an over-cap bonus at entry (illegal value never stored), and `_validate` flags any directly-set skill over the cap so `_cmd_done` blocks finalize. Verified no chargen template exceeds 2D (max authored skill is exactly 2D), so the new cap rejects nothing legitimate. New `tests/test_qa_h7_chargen_skill_cap.py` (7: cap-constant parity, at-cap accepted, over-cap rejected+not-stored, +1-pip boundary, validate flags direct-set, validate passes at-cap, done blocked over-cap). No schema change; era-clean; no faucet/sink; `engine/creation.py` only.

### 2026-06-20 — Onboarding QA: tutorial-chain faction rep was clobbered on every advance — *drop chain-rep-persist*
Closes the **onboarding_chains** QA lane the 2026-06-19 campaign never reached (it died on a session limit). Re-run 2026-06-20 via a break-it-tester walking all 7 starter chains start→graduation through the in-process harness — ONE finding, fixed here. **Bug (CORRUPTION):** completing ANY tutorial chain awarded ZERO faction rep despite the authored step + graduation rewards. `engine/chain_events.py::_try_advance` loads attrs into a local dict; `advance_step` + the graduation/teleport flags mutate THAT dict, but the reward calls (`apply_step_rewards`/`apply_graduation_rewards`→`adjust_rep`) write `faction_rep` straight into `char["attributes"]` (+DB), NOT the local dict — then the function's final blanket `_persist_attrs(db, char, attrs)` wrote the stale local dict back, erasing every chain's rep. Affected all rep-awarding chains (republic_soldier/intelligence, separatist_commando/agent, bounty_hunter, smuggler, shipwright_trader); credits/items/drop-room/chain-state were unaffected. **Fix:** snapshot attrs before the advance, then MERGE-persist — re-read the post-reward `char["attributes"]` and overlay only the keys THIS function changed (chain-state advance + pending teleport/graduation flags, incl. graduation key deletions), so both the rep awards and the advance survive; robust to whatever the reward path writes. Verified: all 7 walkthroughs still graduate (advance unaffected) + a functional walk confirmed rep now persists (republic_soldier ≥6). New `tests/test_chain_rep_persist.py` guard. No schema; era-clean; `engine/chain_events.py` only.

### 2026-06-20 — QA MEDIUM: ghost combat round — pose-grace timer cancelled on combat removal — *drop qa-m-ghost-combat-timer* (Sonnet loop)
`parser/combat_commands.py:_remove_combat` never cancelled `combat._grace_timer_handle` before removing the instance. When combat ended via auto-resolve while the pose-window timer was still running (spawned by `_start_posing_window`), the background task kept sleeping, then fired into the dead/removed combat — broadcasting a spurious pose-nudge message at 90s and calling `_flush_action_log` at 180s, which triggered a ghost initiative roll. Fix: `_remove_combat` now calls `handle.cancel()` on the task handle (via `getattr(combat, '_grace_timer_handle', None)`) before the NPC-behavior cleanup, matching the existing cancel in `_on_pose_submitted`. `asyncio.CancelledError` is already handled in `_pose_grace_timer` (`except asyncio.CancelledError: pass`). No schema change; era-clean; no faucet/sink; `parser/combat_commands.py` only. 6 tests (`tests/test_qa_m_ghost_combat_timer.py`).

### 2026-06-20 — QA HIGH batch 2: H9 buy-order escrow trap + H10 bounty funnel-bypass + H13 error-text leak + H14 harness inventory crash — *drop qa-highs-batch2* (Opus loop)
Four confirmed-still-broken HIGH / test-infra findings from `QA_PLAYTHROUGH_FINDINGS_2026-06-19.md`, each grep-verified at HEAD before fixing. (1) **H9 — `engine/vendor_droids.py:post_buy_order`**: `RESOURCE_TYPES` is a *set*, so the guard `list(RESOURCE_TYPES.keys()) if hasattr(...) else []` produced `[]` → the `and valid_types` short-circuit made the check dead → a `shop order <garbage> …` escrowed real credits into a permanently unfillable order. Fixed to `list(RESOURCE_TYPES)` (yields a set/frozenset/list's elements, a dict's keys). (2) **H10 — `parser/bounty_commands.py:BountyTrackCommand`**: rolled a flat 2D and bypassed the dice funnel — `get_skill_pool()` was called without the required registry (TypeError swallowed → 2D floor) then `roll_d6_pool` directly. Now ranks search/streetwise/tracking by pool and resolves through `perform_skill_check` (wound penalties, lead/tool bonuses, telemetry), mirroring the sister `BountyCollectCommand`. (3) **H13 — `parser/commands.py:CommandParser._execute`**: the catch-all sent raw `str(e)` (Python/SQL/JSON internals) to the player channel; now a generic player line, full detail still via `log.exception`. (4) **H14 — `tests/harness.py:give_item`**: `inv.append(item)` crashed on dict-form inventory (`{"items":[…],"resources":[…]}`), masking real defects; now mirrors `db.add_to_inventory` via `coerce_inventory`. New `tests/test_qa_highs_batch2_2026_06_20.py` (7 tests). No schema change; era-clean; H9 keeps the existing credit-chokepoint escrow path (no new faucet/sink).

### 2026-06-20 — QA LOW: `_pool_to_str` phantom import + `_build_area_contacts` live-dict race — *drop qa-low-pool-str-session-contacts* (Sonnet loop)
Two small QA-LOW fixes. (1) **`engine/skill_checks.py`**: added `_pool_to_str(dice, pips) → str` — the inverse of `_parse_dice_str`, now the canonical home in `skill_checks` (same module, single import point). `parser/medical_commands.py:_get_pool_str` imported it but the symbol didn't exist — `ImportError` was swallowed by `except Exception` and returned "?" instead of the healer's dice pool (e.g., "3D+1"). Now healer dice show correctly on the `heal` offer message. (2) **`server/session.py:_build_area_contacts`**: changed `session_mgr._sessions.values()` to `session_mgr.all()` — the `SessionManager.all()` method returns a snapshot `list`, preventing a `RuntimeError` if a session disconnects mid-iteration (was caught by `except Exception` and blanked the area contacts). New `tests/test_qa_low_pool_str_session_contacts.py` (10 tests). No schema change; era-clean; no faucet/sink.
### 2026-06-20 — QA HIGH H8 (+ adjacent M): combat CP can't be over-spent, floored, and now persisted — *drop qa-h8-combat-cp*
**H8** — declaring multiple CP-spending actions in one combat round validated each action's `cp_spend` against the CURRENT CP, not the RUNNING SUM (`engine/combat.py::declare_action`), so two 5-CP actions with 5 CP on hand both passed and the resolvers (`:1407` ranged / `:1542` melee) subtracted with no floor → `character_points = -5`. Fix: (a) `declare_action` now validates the running sum of `cp_spend` across ALL actions declared this round (rejects the second overcommit with a clear "N already committed this round" message); (b) both resolvers floor at 0 (`max(0, ...)`) as defense-in-depth. **Adjacent M** (combat CP never persisted) — `parser/combat_commands.py` synced `wound_level` to the DB after combat but NOT `character_points`, so CP spent on combat bonuses was refunded on reconnect (a CP-dup exploit); now persists `character_points` (the authoritative floored in-memory value) alongside `wound_level`. New `tests/test_qa_h8_combat_cp.py` (4: functional running-sum rejects the 2nd overcommit, over-budget single rejected, within-budget OK, floor+persist source guards). 71 combat/smoke tests green. `engine/combat.py` is the Opus loop's AVOID-LANE so this is main-session-owned; CP stays floored; era-clean.

### 2026-06-20 — Building INTERIOR maps wired LIVE: Jedi Temple, Coruscant Works, Gladiator Barracks — *drop interiors-wired-2026-06-20*
Adopts the proven Nano interior pipeline as a live feature (Brian 2026-06-20: "do interiors if it adds to the game"). The 3 building interiors whose room slugs appear in NO existing city map — so binding is collision-free — are wired as real tier-1a AreaGeometries (the `senate_district` pattern, fully data-driven via `AreaGeometryRegistry.load_era`; NO renderer change): each ships `data/worlds/clone_wars/maps/<b>.yaml` (the planet's real interior room slugs + districts + exit-graph corridors + landmark chambers) + a painted `static/maps/<b>_substrate.png` (Opus-picked Nano candidate). On entering one of these rooms the registry binds the slug → the interior area and the client renders the painted floorplan + the live nav overlay (room click-targets, movement paths, labeled landmark pins) — where there was previously NO map. **jedi_temple** (11 rooms, hand-authored zone-map, substrate cand_00), **coruscant_works** (4, industrial sublevel, cand_01), **gladiator_barracks** (6, rock-cut compound, cand_00). The 6 OTHER seedable interiors (Kamino cloning-halls/admin, Geonosis hive/foundry/arena, Mos Eisley cantina) are deliberately NOT wired — their rooms already live in a city map, so a second area claiming the same slugs would make navigation nondeterministic (kept as reviewable drafts under `static/tools/batches/_review/`). Tooling: `tools/make_interior_zonemap.py` projects a planet's interior rooms (`map_x`/`map_y`) into a floorplan zone-map (now emits the loader-required per-room `zone`); `tools/_wire_interiors.py` selects + wires + validates. New `tests/test_interior_maps_wired.py` (4): each loads + carries its substrate + every slug binds to its own area (no collision). Verified: all 3 load+validate, all 21 room slugs resolve to live DB rooms, and 118 map/area/registry/map-safety/smoke tests green. Additive (3 new map YAMLs + 3 PNGs + 1 test); era-clean; no engine/renderer change.
### 2026-06-20 — QA HIGH H11: mail sidebar permanently dark — SQL table/column name fix — *drop h11-mail-sidebar-sql* (Sonnet loop)
`session._hud_sidebar_mail` used three wrong identifiers in its SQL query — `mail_messages` (table), `mr.message_id`, `m.sender_name` — none of which exist in the live schema. The resulting `OperationalError` was swallowed in `send_hud_update` (`except Exception: pass`) so `mail_status` WS events never fired and the client `handleMailStatus` was never called → mail sidebar was permanently dark for ALL players. Fix: corrected all three identifiers to the real schema names (`mail`, `mr.mail_id`, `LEFT JOIN characters c ON c.id = m.sender_id` → `c.name as from_name`), matching the exact pattern used by `parser/mail_commands.py:126–131`. New `tests/test_h11_mail_sidebar_sql.py` (8 tests: no-crash, unread count, message fields, system-mail sender_id=0, deleted excluded, unread-first ordering, LIMIT 5 enforced, empty inbox). No schema change; no faucet/sink; era-clean; server/session.py only.

### 2026-06-20 — QA HIGH: phantom `_parse_dice_str` import family — *drop qa-h-phantom-dice-parser*
Fixes the phantom-import HIGH from `docs/design/QA_PLAYTHROUGH_FINDINGS_2026-06-19.md` (Opus loop, the 8-HIGHs lane). Four NPC bargain/gambling call sites — `parser/sabacc_commands.py:132` (dealer gambling pool), `parser/builtin_commands.py:3790` + `:3916` (vendor bargain, buy + sell), `parser/space_commands.py:4184` (planet-vendor bargain) — read an NPC's dice-code off its `char_sheet_json` via `from engine.skill_checks import _parse_dice_str`. But the function lived ONLY in `engine/lightsaber_construction.py`, so every one of those imports raised `ImportError`, was swallowed by the surrounding `except Exception`, and the NPC pool silently fell back to a flat default (DEALER dice for sabacc, 3D for bargains) — NPC Bargain/Gambling skills never mattered. **The callers were right; the function just wasn't there.** Fix: `_parse_dice_str` now has its canonical home in `engine/skill_checks.py` (the module all four callers already targeted; total-by-design — returns `(0,0)` on any anomaly rather than raising, which the swallow-prone sites need), and `engine/lightsaber_construction.py` re-imports it from there (single source of truth — proven identical impl, no behavior change to the lightsaber skill-floor path). Zero edits to the four call sites — they resolve correctly the moment `skill_checks` exports the name. No circular-import risk (verified: `skill_checks` does not import `lightsaber_construction`). No schema, no faucet/sink, era-clean, funnel-respecting (the parsed pool feeds existing `resolve_bargain_check` / dealer-pool paths). 13 tests (`tests/test_qa_h_phantom_dice_parser.py`): canonical-home resolves, single-source-of-truth identity, parse cases incl. `+2D`/bare-int/garbage/whitespace, an AST guard that the 4 call sites import from `engine.skill_checks` (not a no-export module), and call-site-module import-clean.

### 2026-06-19 — Guide_18 Jedi Village: authoritative quality pass — Courage 3-way choice + 24h fail lockout, Flesh 6h wall-clock dwell (leavable), Spirit dark-future-self confrontation (4-reject pass / 3-pull Path C / soft-fail reset) (Opus loop) — *drop guide-18-jedi-village*
Opus-owned GUIDES quality pass over **Guide_18 The Jedi Village & Path A/B/C** — the flagship Force-discovery onboarding arc (the only in-Clone-Wars route to playing a Jedi). Cross-checked every Trial/cooldown/path claim vs HEAD (`engine/village_trials.py`, `engine/force_signs.py`, `engine/jedi_gating.py`, `engine/village_choice.py`, `data/worlds/clone_wars/wilderness/dune_sea.yaml`). The guide carried dense **test-invisible** mechanical drift on three of the five Trials:
- **Trial of Courage rewritten.** Guide taught a "multi-turn dialogue" where "easy answers fail / costly answers pass." Reality: Mira delivers a recital, then a single 3-way choice via `trial courage 1|2|3` — `1` ("I won't deny it.") and `2` ("How did you know?") **both pass** (`COURAGE_PASS_CHOICES == (1, 2)`); only `3` (walk away) fails. The test is engage-vs-walk-away, not clever-line selection. **Fail lockout corrected 14-day → 24-hour** (`COURAGE_FAIL_COOLDOWN_SECONDS == 86_400`; "Come back tomorrow"); the 14-day cooldown only gates the gap between *successful* Trials.
- **Trial of Flesh rewritten.** Guide said "you cannot leave; if you leave the room, the Trial fails and you wait the 14-day cooldown." Reality: a **6-hour wall-clock dwell measured from first cave entry** (`FLESH_DURATION_SECONDS == 21_600`, anchored at `village_trial_flesh_started_at`) — Korvas explicitly tells the player *"You may leave the caves; the discipline continues. You may log out; the discipline continues."* No fail-on-leave, no cooldown; it completes automatically when 6h have elapsed. Stated the 6h concretely and dropped the false continuous-presence framing.
- **Trial of Spirit rewritten.** Guide framed it as "Yarael presents a temptation scenario" with a binary refuse/accept. Reality: a confrontation with the player's **dark-future self** (a faction-flavored apparition wearing the PC's older face), up to `SPIRIT_MAX_TURNS == 7` turns, with **three** responses each turn (`trial spirit 1` reject / `2` waver / `3` lean in). Three outcomes, count-driven: **pass clean** at `SPIRIT_REJECTIONS_TO_PASS == 4` rejections; **Path C lock** at `SPIRIT_DARK_PULL_TO_LOCK_C == 3` temptation pulls (still records `village_trial_spirit_done = 1` + `village_trial_spirit_path_c_locked = 1`, irreversible); **soft-fail** if neither threshold is met by turn 7 → trial ends unfinished, **no cooldown**, restart by re-entering. The old binary missed the ambivalent option, the thresholds, and the soft-fail.
- **§8 cooldown table completed** (added the 24h Courage fail-lockout and 6h Flesh-dwell rows, clarified the 14-day applies only between *successful* Trials), **§9 failure-states** de-conflated (per-Trial fail behaviour: Skill 1h / Courage 24h / Flesh none / Spirit soft-fail none — none of them is the 14-day inter-Trial gate), **§10 hidden-info** path-lock line corrected ("lean in three times", not "fail Spirit into Path C"), **§12 command table** fixed (`trial flesh` is a real progress command not "implicit"; added `trial courage`/`trial spirit` + their `1|2|3` rows; `examine fragment_<N>`/`accuse fragment_<N>` precise arg form). Pinned vs HEAD (verified clean, unchanged): Hermit's Hut `(33, 16)` west of the Anchor Stones (== `dune_sea.yaml [33, 16]`), 50h/180,000s playtime gate, 5-sign threshold + 0.0028 base sign probability, Skill `craft_lightsaber` 8/12/15 + 1h retry + kyber-crystal reward, 7-day Act-1→Act-2 + 14-day inter-Trial cooldowns, Path A/B/C rewards/teleports (`jedi_temple_main_gate` + Master Tova Resh / `village_common_square` + Independent +50 rep / `dune_sea_anchor_stones` + `dark_path_unlocked` + `dark_contact_freq`). `tests/test_guide_18_jedi_village.py` (16) pins each correction to its live engine constant so a future retune fails loudly here. Docs/test only, engine+data READ-ONLY, era-clean, no schema/faucet-sink, no avoid-lane (`village_trials.py` dark-future-self prophecy untouched — guide-only re-description per the sanctioned-surface rule).

Fixed four real drifts + one era-polish: (1) **§2 "75 skills"→"76"** — the loaded `SkillRegistry` carries 76 (the `Powersuit Operation` Mechanical skill was added 2026-06-13). (2) **§10 phantom "Clone Trooper Armor" (+1D/+2D/−1D Dex)** — no such registry row; those exact stats are the real `improved_armor` ("Improved Body Armor") → renamed the phantom to the real item. (3) **§4 partial-success** said "(missions, repairs, bounties) … by 4 or fewer" — actually system-specific: repairs `margin >= -4`, missions `margin >= -2`, bounties resolve via combat/capture (no margin window) → rewrote to the accurate per-system thresholds, dropped the bounty claim. (4) **§2 `+roll 4D+2` example** showed normal dice "3, 5, 2" — `roll_d6_pool` sorts them **descending** (`reverse=True`) → fixed to "5, 3, 2". (5) **§6 scale examples** Walker "AT-ST, AT-AT" + Capital "Star Destroyer, Mon Calamari cruiser" were GCW-flavored while the Starfighter row was already CW-era (ARC-170, Vulture Droid) → made Walker "AT-TE, AT-RT" + Capital "Venator-class Star Destroyer, Acclamator-class assault ship". Pinned vs HEAD (all verified clean): §3 Wild Die explode/complication, §4 difficulty ladder (5/10/15/20/25/30) == `Difficulty` enum, §6 scale table (0/2/4/6/9/12/18) == `Scale` enum + char-vs-starfighter diff 6, §7 wound penalties + `can_act` ladder + stun-KO (`len(stun_timers) >= str_dice`) == `WoundLevel`/`Character`, §8 CP/FP mechanics, §10 every weapon/melee/armor damage+cost == `weapons.yaml`, §11 data-flow symbols all importable, §1 Human 18D/2D–4D + Wookiee STR 3D–6D/KNO 2D+1 == species yaml. `tests/test_guide_01_core_mechanics.py` (39). Docs/test only, engine+data READ-ONLY, era-clean, no schema/faucet-sink. **FLAGGED follow-ups (engine, NOT done):** (a) `WoundLevel.WOUNDED_TWICE` (−2D) is defined + rendered on the char sheet ("W.Twice") but the combat damage ladder jumps Wounded→Incapacitated, never producing it — latent reachability gap in `engine/character.py` (avoid-lane). (b) `data/species/wookiee.yaml` story_factor "Imperial enslavement of Wookiees is widespread" is a B3 era violation (Imperial in a production string) — kept this drop guide-only per the engine/data-READ-ONLY pattern.

### 2026-06-19 — Guide_17 Player Shops: authoritative quality pass — phantom `bargain` command killed, buy/sell/order syntax corrected, 10% haggle cap, up-front escrow, relist fee, in-place upgrade (Opus loop) — *drop guide-17-player-shops*
Opus-owned GUIDES quality pass over **Guide_17 Player Shops & Trading** (the passive-revenue commerce guide), cross-checked against `engine/vendor_droids.py`, `engine/skill_checks.resolve_bargain_check`, `parser/shop_commands.py`, the customer `buy`/`sell` routers (`parser/space_commands.py` / `parser/builtin_commands.py`) and `data/vendor_droids.yaml`. The guide carried a cluster of test-INVISIBLE command-surface and mechanical drift (the convention invariant guards the registry, not guide prose):
- **PHANTOM `bargain` command killed.** §1/§4/§5/§13 taught `bargain <slot>` as a customer move. There is no `bargain` command at all — the haggle is applied AUTOMATICALLY inside the customer's `buy`, and only on Tier 2+ droids (`buy_from_droid` runs the Bargain check only `if b_dice > 0 or b_pips > 0`). A **Tier 1 droid never haggles** — it sells at the listed price (the guide previously claimed the opposite: that Tier 1 "customers can always haggle prices down").
- **Haggle cap corrected 10-25% → 10%.** `resolve_bargain_check` maps ±2% per 4 points of opposed-roll margin, capped ±10%. The "10-25% off" prose was wrong.
- **Customer buy syntax** `buy <slot> [quantity]` → **`buy <slot#> from <shop name>`** (or item name); `buy_from_droid` has NO quantity param (one unit per buy).
- **Buy-order fulfilment** `sell <qty> to <shop>` → **`sell <resource> to <shop name>`** (resource name; quantity automatic, up to the order's remaining need).
- **Posting a buy order** `shop order <item> <max_price> [qty]` → **`shop order <resource> <min_quality> <qty> <price_per>`** (four args, crafting-resources only). The old `shop order metal 50 100` example would not even parse.
- **Buy orders are resource-only** (validated vs crafting `RESOURCE_TYPES`) — not "buy completed items from other crafters"; **escrow is deducted up front** at post time (full `qty × price_per`), not gradually as customers sell; the **phantom "max 5 simultaneous orders" cap removed** (no count cap exists — escrow is the limiter). Cancelling refunds unspent escrow.
- **Tier upgrade** is `shop upgrade <tier>` IN PLACE (inventory preserved, price difference charged: gn4→gn7 3,000 / gn7→gn12 7,000 / gn4→gn12 10,000 cr) — §1's "buy a new droid, transfer inventory, sell the old one back for a refund" was phantom (no droid-sellback mechanism exists).
- **Documented the live but previously-omitted recurring relisting fee** (1% of slot value, min 10 cr, on listings idle >30 days, daily `vendor_relist_fee` sink) in §4/§9/§14.
- VERIFIED ACCURATE vs HEAD (now pinned): tier costs/slots/fees/bargain pools (`data/vendor_droids.yaml`), 50% price floor (`PRICE_FLOOR_PCT`), 30/60-day warn/recall (`_WARN_DAYS`/`_RECALL_DAYS`), 2/room + 3/owner droid caps, the four forbidden room types + `no_commerce`, `market search [planet|all]` (bare `market` = cargo prices).
- `tests/test_guide_17_player_shops.py` (32) resolves every taught command against the live registry, asserts `bargain` is NOT a command, and pins every number against the engine constants. Docs/test only; engine + data READ-ONLY; era-clean; no schema, no faucet/sink.
- **FLAGGED follow-up (engine, NOT done — possible balance bug):** the `if b_dice > 0 or b_pips > 0` gate means a **Tier 1 droid never engages the haggle**, so it sells at full sticker — likely the *opposite* of the intended "Tier 1 is easy to haggle down, upgrade to protect prices" design. If intended behavior is that Tier 1 has a weak/zero pool customers easily beat (rather than no haggle at all), the gate should let Tier 1 through `resolve_bargain_check` (which floors the NPC pool at 1D). Guide now documents HEAD's actual behavior; left engine untouched (guides are docs-only). Worth a Brian ruling.

### 2026-06-19 — Guide_08 Force Powers: authoritative quality pass (13-power roster restored, Affect Mind de-dark-sided, DSP tiers + advancement corrected, engine cross-check guard) (Opus loop) — *drop guide-08-force-powers*
The Opus-owned guides quality pass over the Force Powers guide, which had drifted badly from HEAD. Verified every command the guide teaches against the SAME live registry `server/game_server` builds and cross-checked the entire power roster, difficulties, dark-side flags, DSP mechanics and advancement path against the live `engine/force_powers` + `engine/character`. **Roster restored (8 → 13):** the guide documented only the original 8 powers; the Drop 4a / 4a.2 expansion (2026-06-04) added **Telepathy** (Sense, Moderate 15), **Sense Deception** (Sense, Moderate 15), **Farseeing** (Sense, Difficult 20) and **Danger Sense** (Sense, Moderate 15), and split the old mind trick into a light **Affect Mind** + a dark **Dominate Mind** (Difficult 20). §1/§2/§3 rewritten to teach all 13 across Control (3) / Sense (6) / Alter (2) / Combination (2). **CRITICAL correction — Affect Mind is no longer dark side:** the guide marked Affect Mind ⚠️ DARK SIDE / "Always earns 1 Dark Side Point", but `affect_mind.dark_side is False` at HEAD — it is the *light* Jedi mind trick (suggestion); the corrupting counterpart is the new **Dominate Mind** (coercion). The two dark powers are now **Injure/Kill** and **Dominate Mind**. Teaching a player that the canonical Jedi mind trick self-corrupts is a real, safety-relevant error the green suite never caught (the convention-invariant test guards the command registry, not guide prose). Fixed §1, §3 and §5 accordingly. **DSP warning tiers (§5) corrected** to match `_dsp_warning`'s actual bands (1–3 generic point note / 4–5 "the darkness grows within you" / 6+ fall check + "the darkness is consuming you") — the old guide had them off by one tier. Added a brief note on the **Weight of War** fall-check modifier (war-weary Jedi resist the fall less; +2/+5/+10 by tier, extra DSP on a failed resist at the top tier) per `WoW.3c`. **Advancement phantom removed (§7):** the guide claimed Control/Sense/Alter "advance the same way as regular skills" via the `train` command with a 1 / 6 / 15 CP table — but `train` only advances `skills.yaml` skills, and Control/Sense/Alter are not skills there (`train control` is rejected). Rewrote §7 to the real path: Force disciplines are awakened at chargen/Jedi-Village trials and developed through the **Master–Padawan `+teach` bond** (Padawan's CP, guild/bond discount), cross-referencing Guide #14. **Command canonicalization:** §3/§8 now teach `+powers`/`+forcestatus` (A1: OOC/query gets the `+` prefix; bare `powers`/`forcestatus` survive as live aliases). **Telekinesis disarm corrected** from the flavor-string "opposed by their Dexterity" to the real mechanic (beat the difficulty by a margin of 3+, per `DISARM_MARGIN`). New `tests/test_guide_08_force_powers.py` (68): every taught command resolves; the engine roster, each power's difficulty + dark-side flag, the DSP fall threshold, the disarm margin and the not-a-trainable-skill fact are all cross-checked against HEAD so a future engine retune that desyncs the guide fails loudly; the Affect-Mind-is-light and no-`train`-phantom corrections are pinned. Docs/content + test only; no engine logic, no schema, no faucet/sink, era-clean; `force_powers.py`/`force_commands.py`/`character.py`/`cp_commands.py` read-only (engine untouched).

### 2026-06-19 — Guide_04 Security Zones: authoritative quality pass (phantom +25% lawless CP bonus removed, @security/territory refs corrected, +pvp documented, engine cross-check guard) (Opus loop) — *drop guide-04-security-zones*
The Opus-owned guides quality pass over the Security Zones guide (the EVE-style Secured/Contested/Lawless layer that gates all combat). Verified every command the guide teaches against the SAME live registry `server/game_server` builds and cross-checked every quantified mechanic against the live engine. **Phantom removed:** §6 + §9 promised a **"+25% CP tick-rate bonus while in a lawless zone"** — no such modifier exists. `engine/cp_engine` has exactly four income sources (passive trickle / scene bonus / kudos / AI evaluator) and is entirely zone-blind; standing in a lawless room earns no CP at all. Rewrote both passages to state CP accrues from *play* (missions, scenes, kudos) — which dangerous zones host more of — not from loitering. **Command-reference fixes (test-invisible — the convention-invariant test guards the registry, not guide prose):** §8 mischaracterized `@security override <room> = none` as a generic "clear any override" and omitted the actual `@security override <room> = <faction>` **set form** — the `override` subform is a per-room *faction override* (hostile/unfriendly PCs of the named faction see a SECURED room as LAWLESS), not a security-level toggle. Rewrote §8 to teach all four real subforms and the persistence model (admin `@security` zone-sets write the DB → durable; Director surges/crackdowns are in-memory → reset on restart). §7 still described the **retired per-room** claim model; corrected to the live **per-region** wilderness ownership (`faction claim`; LAWLESS→CONTESTED citadel upgrade for the owning org's members; non-members and independents see base; ceiling is CONTESTED, never SECURED). **Completeness (Opus depth pass):** §2 expanded from "four things" to the full resolution set — added the **room faction-override** (#5) and **player-city citizen upgrade** (#6, CONTESTED→SECURED / LAWLESS→CONTESTED for citizens) factors the engine actually applies in `_finalize`; §3 now documents the **`+pvp` self-flag** (open PvP in CONTESTED only, never overrides SECURED, 5-minute anti-tag-and-flee cooldown) the guide previously omitted; §6 softened the "rare resources ONLY in lawless" overstatement (Contested/Control rooms also carry a T5-rare chance per the harvest yield table). **Mechanics verified accurate against HEAD (now pinned):** §3 challenge TTL = `_PVP_CHALLENGE_TTL` 600s (10 min) + `+pvp` unflag = `PVP_UNFLAG_COOLDOWN_S` 300s (5 min); §2 influence thresholds (underworld ≥80 downgrade / authority ≥75 upgrade / authority ≥90 martial-law forced-SECURED) match `_apply_director_overlay` behaviorally; §5 space-tier mapping (DOCK→secured, ORBIT/HYPERSPACE→contested, DEEP_SPACE→lawless) matches `_SPACE_SECURITY_BY_TYPE`; §7 citadel upgrade matches `_apply_wilderness_ownership`; §4 `+bounty/claim` resolves (umbrella `+bounty`, switch `claim`). New `tests/test_guide_04_security_zones.py` (27): every taught command resolves, the phantom stays dead (no `+25%` in the guide + `cp_engine` asserted zone-blind), and each numeric claim is cross-checked against the engine so a future retune that desyncs the guide fails loudly. Docs/content + test only; no engine logic, no schema, no faucet/sink, era-clean; `security.py`/`cp_engine.py`/`combat_commands.py`/`harvest.py` read-only (avoid-lane untouched).

### 2026-06-19 — SpaceGrid boot rehydration (LOW verify finding — ships visible after restart) — *drop spacegrid-boot-rehydration*
Fixes the LOW finding from `VERIFY_FINDINGS_2026-06-18.md`: after a server restart, the in-memory `SpaceGrid` was rebuilt empty — undocked, realspace ships were absent from the combat/range/targeting grid until each pilot explicitly relaunched, meaning any session that began shortly after a restart had broken targeting and combat-range for ships that were already in space. Fix: `game_server.start()` now queries `db.get_ships_in_space()` (non-docked rows) immediately before starting the network listeners, filters out ships in hyperspace (correctly absent until `hyperspace_arrival_tick` re-adds them on exit), and calls `self.space_grid.add_ship()` for each realspace ship, mirroring the exact pattern used by `hyperspace_arrival_tick`. Per-ship JSON parse is guarded (`try/except JSONDecodeError`) so one malformed systems blob can't abort the whole rehydration block; the outer try/except makes the whole step fail-open (log warning, game boots). New `tests/test_spacegrid_boot_rehydration.py` (10 tests): basic add-ship/empty-grid, realspace ship added at correct speed, hyperspace ship skipped, mixed fleet, unknown-template fallback speed (5), empty ship list, malformed JSON gracefully treated as empty dict, hyperspace-arrival add-ship non-regression, get_ships_in_space drift guard (SQL must exclude `docked_at IS NULL`). Server/game-server only; no schema, no faucet/sink, era-clean, no avoid-lane. (Sonnet loop)

### 2026-06-19 — Guide_03 Ground Combat: authoritative quality pass (2 broken combat-command references fixed + engine cross-check guard) (Opus loop) — *drop guide-03-ground-combat*
The Opus-owned guides quality pass over the largest, most-played guide (Ground Combat, 38 KB). Verified **every** combat command the guide teaches against the SAME live registry `server/game_server` builds, and cross-checked the §4/§5/§7/§9/§11/§14 mechanics tables against the live engine constants. **Two test-INVISIBLE broken command references fixed** (the convention-invariant test guards the registry, not free-text guide prose, so the unit suite couldn't see these): **(1) §13 posing** taught `> pose <text>` to submit a combat pose — but bare `pose` is the generic room-emote alias (`EmoteCommand` key `emote`, aliases `:`/`pose`/`em`); it broadcasts an ordinary emote and never registers as the round's combat pose, silently leaving the player with the auto-pose. Fixed to the real command **`cpose <text>`** (`CombatPoseCommand`, alias `combatpose`), with an explicit teaching note distinguishing it from the bare `pose`/`:` emote. **(2) §16 quick reference** listed `force-point` (hyphenated) — the registered key is `forcepoint` (aliases `fp`/`+fp`), no hyphenated alias exists, so `force-point` resolved to nothing; fixed to `forcepoint` (or `fp`). Also added the missing `cpose` quick-ref row, aligned the `crolls`/`combat rolls` and `cover [quarter|half|3/4|full]` rows to the engine's actual vocabulary. **Mechanics verified accurate against HEAD (no change needed, now pinned):** §5 damage-margin → wound bands (1–3 Stunned / 4–8 Wounded / 9–12 Incapacitated / 13–15 Mortally Wounded / 16+ Dead) match `WoundLevel.from_damage_margin` at every boundary; §4/§7 cover dice (+1D/+2D/+3D for 1/4·1/2·3/4) match `COVER_QUARTER`/`COVER_HALF`/`COVER_THREE_QUARTER`; §9 aim cap (+3D) matches `min(actor.aim_bonus + 1, 3)`; §11 NPC-AI table lists exactly the five live `CombatBehavior` profiles (aggressive/defensive/cowardly/berserk/sniper); §14 mortal-wound death roll (2D, die if total < rounds mortally wounded) matches `engine/combat.py`. New `tests/test_guide_03_ground_combat.py` (29): every taught command resolves, both fixes pinned (no `force-point`, no bare `> pose` instruction, `cpose` taught), and each mechanics table cross-checked against the engine so a future retune that desyncs the guide fails loudly. Docs/content + test only; no engine logic, no schema, no faucet/sink, era-clean; combat.py/character.py/npc_combat_ai.py read-only (avoid-lane untouched).

**QA L3 (QA_FINDINGS_2026-06-16.md)** found that `advance_skill()` contained a dead if-branch and a docstring claiming "cost doubled above attribute" — but the code never doubles (WEG R&E rule: cost = current total dice, period). The `advance_skill` fix + tests landed earlier (the source no longer says "doubled", the dead branch is gone). This drop closes the **remaining L3 artifact**: the `parser/cp_commands.py` **module docstring** at line 15 still said `"train costs current_dice CP (doubled if above attribute)"` — wrong, and unchecked by the existing L3 tests (which scope to `Character.advance_skill`). ### 2026-06-19 — In-game `Type 'X'` command hints: post-rework breakage sweep + durable guard (Opus loop) — *drop ingame-hint-resolve*
The command-syntax rework (Drops 0-7) deleted the bare query/meta forms and made the `+`-prefixed variant canonical. The guide-syntax guards swept player-facing **guide prose**, but the dozens of imperative `Type 'X'` hints emitted from **engine/parser code in live play** were an unguarded surface — a hint that tells a new player to `Type 'missions'` when the bare form was deleted is a "command not found" the unit suite can't see (the convention-invariant test guards the registry, not free-text hint strings). Audited every `Type 'X'` hint in `engine/`/`parser/`/`server/` against the SAME live registry `server/game_server` builds (resolving the base word through aliases + `+cmd/<switch>` bases). Of 30+ hints, the bulk resolve fine (`help`/`?`/`commands` are sanctioned `+help` aliases the rework kept; bare combat verbs `attack`/`dodge`/`aim`/`flee`/`cover`/`range` are registered at their bare keys; `missions`/`bounties`/`powers`/`weapons`/etc. resolve via alias). **Two were genuinely broken and are fixed:** (1) **`engine/spacer_quest.py`** step-8 hint `Type 'factions'` → `Type '+factions'` — bare `factions` was deleted by the rework, so every new spacer following the sector-intel hint hit a dead command. (2) **`parser/space_commands.py`** `@spawn` unknown-template error pointed admins at a nonexistent `Type 'ships'` command → now lists the real available template keys from the in-process registry (`", ".join(sorted(t.key for t in reg.all_templates()))`), non-phantom discovery using the existing `ShipRegistry.all_templates()` API. **Documented non-breakages:** `boarding_link`/`boarding_link_back` are movement EXITS (`engine/boarding.py` `BOARDING_EXIT_DIR_TO`/`_FROM`), resolved by the movement system not the command registry — you cross a boarding link by typing the exit name like `north`; allowlisted. **Tech-debt flagged:** `engine/tutorial.py` (v1 `TutorialManager`) is instantiated at `game_server.py:454` but **never driven** (no `start`/`advance`/`skip` call site anywhere) — superseded by the chain-tutorial system selected at chargen; its `Type 'skip tutorial'` hints are unreachable dead code (the real `training skip` is itself disabled). Excluded from the guard pending removal (`TODO.json` `tech_debt.tutorial_v1_dead_code`). New `tests/test_ingame_command_hints_resolve.py` (4): every live `Type 'X'` hint resolves against the registry (caught **2 additional** would-be false-positive data-type docstrings — `objects` rows `of type 'breachable'` — excluded by a precise regex), allowlist entries are genuinely not commands, + regression pins on both fixes. Chargen-internal hints (`creation.py`/`creation_wizard.py` free-form loop) are excluded — that vocabulary is its own input loop, guarded separately. String/docs + test only; no schema, no faucet/sink, era-clean; no avoid-lane file touched.

### 2026-06-19 — Verify-campaign MEDIUM fixes: rate-bucket address-reuse + IP-throttle empty-key leak — *drop verify-fixes-mem-leaks*
Three memory/correctness fixes from `VERIFY_FINDINGS_2026-06-18.md` MEDIUM findings (Sonnet loop). **(1) Parser rate-bucket address-reuse fix (`parser/commands.py`).** `CommandParser._check_rate_limit` keyed its per-session token bucket on `id(session)` — the CPython memory address, which is reused after GC. A new session created at the same address inherited the previous session's drained bucket, causing cross-session rate-limit bleed (new players briefly unable to type fast). Fixed: key on `session.id` (monotonically increasing `Session._next_id`, never reused). Added `CommandParser.clear_session(session_id)` to remove the stale entry on disconnect. Wired the cleanup into `GameServer` at all three session-removal sites (kicked-existing on token-auth, kicked-existing on password-auth, and normal session teardown). **(2) IP-throttle empty-key leak (`server/api.py`).** `_sliding_window_allow` used `bucket[ip]` (defaultdict — creates the key on first access) and never deleted the key when pruning left it empty. Over time every distinct IP that ever hit a throttled endpoint accumulated a stale empty-list key. Fixed: use `bucket.get(ip, [])` instead (no phantom key creation) and `bucket.pop(ip, None)` when pruning leaves the list empty. This fix covers all three throttle dicts that route through `_sliding_window_allow`: the strict chargen-write limiter (`_rate_limits`), the soft read-endpoint limiter (`_soft_rate_limits`), and the pre-auth connect/create limiter (`_preauth_attempts` in `game_server.py`, which imports this function). **(3) Portal login-throttle empty-key leak (`server/web_portal.py`).** `_login_rate_ok` had the same inline pattern. Fixed to match. New `tests/test_verify_mem_leaks.py` (12 tests): key-delete-on-expiry, no-phantom-key-on-first-get, rate-limit-at-max (sliding window), login-rate cleanup, CommandParser keyed-on-session-id not address, clear_session no-op for unknown id. No schema, no faucet/sink, era-clean, no avoid-lane.
